<Content>Just the best location MY husband and I and our two daughters have just returned from a 5 week trip the to the United States. Our last stop was Hawaii. This was the first time for all of us. We stayed 7 nights at the ResortQuest Waikki Circle Hotel. It was just fantastic.When we arrived at the hotel the reception people were just delightful and couldn't do enough to help. It was like family. In some of the larger hotels we had stayed in throughtout the states you were just another number.The room we had was on the 12th floor with an ocean view. Although it wasn't oceanfront it was beautiful. Loved the decor of the room. The balconies were great to sit morning and night.A complete surprise was the free coffee each morning in the lobby from 6.45am - 9.00am. A daily newspaper delivered to your door each morning.Great shampoo/conditioner and soaps in the bathroom each day.McDonalds was right next door which was handy with young children. There were shops and restaurants everywhere in the area. The ABC shops were just fantastic being on every corner. They are reasonably priced as well. The International Market Place was a short walk. The Zoo also a short walk in the opposite direction. Tour desk was very helpful.We have been back in Sydney for 1 week and we have already decided that we would love to go back for 3 weeks this year and spend Xmas again and extend to New Year. It was just the best location and a wonderful way to finish off our holiday.

<Author>juanitaIndiana
<Content>Such a deal! Absolutely, positively the most wonderful hotel experience in Waikiki. Reserved ocean front room and stayed in Room 404 first night. Requested to be relocated to a higher floor room by 2nd day and staff graciously moved all our luggage up to Room 1306 while we were busy sightseeing. Unbelievable ocean view from room! Rooms were small, but caused no problem since we could unpack suitcases and place contents on closet shelves, hangers in closet, or in small bureau under TV. Bathroom space was fine and shower water pressure was fantastic. Rooms were very clean and beds were fabulous. Best location in Waikiki and very SAFE area with police station just across street. Super clean beach across street with free cultural entertainment nightly. Staff were extremely friendly and laid back. Lobby also has a tour company representative behind another counter, who was quite helpful in arranging excellent day trips. The Circle was definitely a throwback to the 50's and 60's era, which was quite refreshing amongst all the high rise hotels, condos, and name brand shops. The ABC store next door was convenient and somewhat reasonably priced. McDonalds was a great stop for early morning coffee on the way to sunrise and surfer viewing across the street on the beach. Doesn't get much better!

<Author>Butterflystomper
<Content>Will definitely come back here! We spent 3 days of our 10 day stay at the Circle. We arrived late at the airport (10:30 pm) and hopped on the Airport Shuttle ($8.00 one way), the driver turned on a Hawaiin CD and we were off and a few stops later dropped at our hotel. There were 5 in our party so we had two oceanfront rooms on the 8th floor, I had asked for 7th floor or higher on the advice from TripAdvisor reviews. We were not disappointed - the views are fantastic, the accommodation is comfortable, plenty of towels, shampoo, soaps and lotions, room safe ($2.50 a day but gives you great piece of mind when you leave your passport etc behind), each with a balcony. Hula shows directly across the street and our last night a lone street musician playing guitar on the beach with his music floating up to our room. This spot is perfect - at the break of dawn people are out running, jogging, strolling, walking the dog, on their way to work, heading for the beach and you can watch the city start to come alive. All this while laying in bed reading your morning paper delivered to your door and drinking complimentary coffee supplied in the lobby each morning. The staff are very friendly and well informed. Even after checkout they will lock up your luggage until you are ready to leave the city. They provide use of beach toys, towels, you can lock up your surf board if you bring it with you all with a safe swimming beach directly across the street. We had two teenagers with us and they loved going to the International Marketplace, picking up a quick bite to eat, or strolling the beach on their own and could easily find their way back to the hotel. Everything is a short walk away. There was no room noise at all from other visitors and the rooms catch the ocean breezes. I would definitely recommend this hotel with its funky, relaxed ambience, great staff and location.  
<Date>Nov 19, 2008

<Author>Harleynut
<Content>I'm Home! Just returned from a 3 week U.S.A. trip topped off with 5 days in Hawaii. We had stayed at The Circle 18 months ago and had been eager to return. We arrived at 8.00am from Vegas and checked in immediately. I was half-expecting a problem with the bookings because were using Entertainment Book Cards for a 50% discount, but all was correct  efficient. We were warmly welcomed and offered hot coffee. Obviously the rooms weren't ready, but the staff were happy to store our luggage  supply an area where we could change  freshen up. The girls took off for the shops for the day  the boys hired a couple of mopeds to do a bit of exploring. We returned around 3.30pm  the rooms were ready. Staff had changed shift and were as pleasant as the previous. A young porter eagerly organised our luggage and escorted us to our room. Imagine my surprise to be escorted to the same room we stayed in on our last visit. Room 805 - what a top spot! Beautiful views from this baby. Some friends that were staying at the Sheraton Princess stopped in for a couple of drinks on our lanai one night and announced Now this is THE SPOT. We smiled  nodded. They were paying nearly 4x what we were. Sure, their room was larger  they had a pool, but they wished they could swap with us. No way!Rooms were the same as last visit. You've heard it before:2 double beds, minifridge, desk  chair, safe, LCD tv on top of small chest of drawers, small mirrored wardrobe in end of alcove, wall air conditioner, small bathroom with shower only, 2 chairs  a drinks table on the lanai. No coffeemaking facilities in the room. It's ABC store next door or free coffee from the lobby in the morning. Want a pool? There's a huge one with waves out the front door and don't forget to pick up your free towel at the front desk.All of this was clean  tidy and housekeeping made sure it stayed that way for the duration of our stay. I was a bit off colour and slept quite late one morning during the usual housekeeping time. No problem. They returned in a few hours  tidied up while we relaxed on the lanai, finishing in just a few minutes. Should you need a laundry, there is one 2 blocks directly behind The Circle, coin-operated  it takes quarters. Our stay was as great as the first one and we look forward with enthusiasm to our next stay. The units are clean, comfortable budget accomodation on the inside and the best Hawaii has to offer your eyes from your lanai. Don't expect the Hilton - it's not. There's scratches  stains, chips  flakes. She's an honest old lady with a friendly feel. The only complaint I had was the aching pain I felt as I grudgingly boarded the airport shuttle.

<Author>Johnsy
<Content>You Get Exactly What You Pay For My husband and I have just come back from our very first overseas trip to Hawaii and stayed at the Circle for 6 nights.On arrival, we were given a room on the 4th floor and asked to be upgraded to a room a bit higher. Unfortunately they were booked out, but were able to move us to the 10th floor 2 nights later. If you are booking this place, make sure that you pay the extra money for an oceanfront room, it is so worth it. If you don't, you may not be able to upgrade as I think that the secret is out about this place, and it may be booked out. We spoke to other Aussies staying here, and they had all tried to upgrade unsuccessfully as there were no rooms left.Anyway, as others have said, view is to die for. You would struggle to get this view anywhere else in Waikiki for the money that we paid. It is lovely just sitting on the balcony and watching the world go by.The rooms are exceptionally clean, beds are very comfortable, the in room safe is handy to leave your valuables when you don't want to carry them around, but the room is very basic and very small. We didn't mind as we knew this from reading trip advisor reviews, but if you are looking for a bit of luxury you wouldn't stay here.We didn't find any noise from the rooms around us or from the street below, but we always pack our earplugs and we were so tired from being on the go all day that we just slept like logs.I agree with the previous poster that Vicki on the tour desk is fantastic. Nothing was too much trouble and she ended up treating us like family. I quite enjoyed the Kona Coffee that the Circle provides free for guests every morning, and we made use of the free beach towels every day.All in all, you get what you pay for here - a 2 and a half star room that is very clean but very small, but what makes this place worth every penny is the 5 star view.  
<Date>Nov 11, 2008

<Author>LaraH19
<Content>A tale of two hotels! A Tale of 2 Hotels!October 20th 2008The 鈥渇irst鈥?hotel is located in such a prime location you would expect to be paying huge prices, however the rates here were very reasonable. It is within a few steps of an ABC store in either direction so that gives you the opportunity of purchasing breakfast provisions daily, to eat at the beach or on the balcony if you prefer. It is directly across the road from the beach so in a few seconds you can be in the water or lazing on the sand, lying underneath an umbrella if you wish to pay the small hire fee. The hotel provides good beach towels which is very convenient, and saves on luggage space.The view is to die for, especially if there is a brilliant sunset, and to have an oceanfront room here is certainly one of the best views you will get in Waikiki. I am very fussy about cleanliness and this hotel meets my requirements and the toiletries are very nice, we even asked for additional and this was supplied without question.The beds are very comfortable, and the additional pillows we requested were placed in our room as soon as our backs were turned. The water supply is efficient and we enjoyed long hot showers. Fortunately, the towels are plentiful.As this is not a large hotel we had no time wasted waiting for lifts and there was always one available.The tour desk consultant, Vicki, was so friendly and knowledgeable; she was a real pleasure to deal with. Her contacts meant that our tours were fantastic and it was so easy to make them on site without the hassle of finding someone we could trust along the street front.The fridge was very efficient and meant that we could store our drinks and snacks to enjoy on our balcony each evening.The 鈥渙ther鈥?hotel we stayed at was very different. There was constant noise from people down in the street below all hours of the night and deliveries very early in the morning, even though we were on the 10th floor. Also, the noise from adjoining rooms indicated that the walls are very thin.The room is very small and we were never told that there was an option of a 鈥渒ing size bed only鈥?room, esp when we were just a couple. If you are in a room with 2 double beds, and anymore than 2 suitcases, you will find limited room to move around.The shower is small so if you are on the large size do not expect to have much room to lift your arms to wash, and the flimsy shower curtain does not prevent water getting all over the floor.Do not expect to be able to fit anymore than one person in the bathroom at a time, the sink juts out and makes a midnight dash slightly dangerous as there is not much room to maneuver. The shower towels are very, very thin, requiring the need to use several each time.By now I must explain that the 2 hotels are actually one in the same, just polar points apart! If money is no object then I鈥檇 assume you would not be making this hotel you choice of accommodation anyway. If you are budget conscious and prefer to allocate your holiday dollar elsewhere then this hotel may just be perfect. Also, many who holiday here do not spend much time in their room at all and if it is just to sleep at the end of another day in paradise, then this hotel would be quite appropriate.

<Author>CedricJ
<Content>Best Value in Waikiki My wife and I recently stayed at this hotel for 3 wonderful nights. This was our second visit to the Circle (and Honolulu) and once again, could find little fault.Yes the rooms are small but the convenience of staying in a hotel directly across from Waikiki beach with unobstructed views at the price they charge makes this hotel a little gem. The position of the hotel is perfect being right in the middle of the beach area.The staff and service are excellent. I'd hate to think how long it would have taken if this was a 500 room hotel instead of 100.Our favourite restaurant in Waikiki by the way, is the Californian Pizza Kitchen. <Author>missemilydiana
<Content>Incredible View and Cute Little Hotel We loved the Waikiki Circle Hotel! I personally was really impressed with the history of the hotel and we really appreciated the little extras more than anything - really incredible shower soap, wonderful smelling lotion, the cute little fish next to the sink which we kept to remember our stay with, and the great seperate shampoo and condition. Most hotels these days provide low-grade extras that you wouldn't use unless you had to and you definitely would not take home, but I took home the items and I would actually love to be able to purchase more. The tour desk left something to be desired, the lady had kind of a thick accent and she was really brief when we asked questions so we just went off of our own ideas. The beds were comfortable and the shower heads had good pressure and were very functional. Plus you get a mini-fridge at no extra cost so that you can eat leftovers the next morning. You also get free coffee in the morning at 6:45 AM until 9 AM and it's delicious Kona coffee. All of the front desk clerks could tell you how to get where you were going and what bus to take. Also, they will hold your bags for you if you arrive before check-in and if you are not leaving until hours after check-out so that you can continue to explore the city. The air conditioning was wonderful. Most of the hotels I read about prior to booking with this one had comments from customers frustrated about the complete lack of air conditioning, but ours was great. We stayed on the top floor and had a ocean front room and the view was absolutely breathtaking. The location of the hotel on the street was great because it was close to Kapahulu where we often ate because of the cheaper prices and more authentic food. I highly recommend this hotel and when I return to Oahu in the future, this is where I am booking. FYI - Do not miss Ono's Hawaiian Restaraunt located just a couple blocks up Kapahulu Street on the left - it was incredible!!! And if you are going to hike diamond head - take the bus or a trolley, don't try to walk there, it's quite a ways. The Bodies exhibit is in town and just a trolley ride away until January 09 and it was really interesting although pricey - $24/adult. Don't take taxis/cabs! You can get a better deal by using the shuttle services that are available - VIP is the company we used most - $8/person from airport to hotel, $8 from hotel to Pearl Harbor, etc. We rode the city bus once and it wasn't a great experience. Do not order the pancakes at Mac 24/7, a restaraunt nearby. They are open literally 24/7 which is nice, but unless you have 5 people in your party, you will never be able to eat the giant pancakes they serve up. LuLu's was a nice restaraunt, although pricey just like all of the others on the strip in front of the beach, and it is just up the street toward diamond head from the hotel. Definitely get a burger from Burger In Paradise, right next to the hotel. Skip Haagan Daaz or other ice cream joints, you end up paying $6-7 for some ice cream. Room 1404 is the best view in the hotel. I will try to upload some photos later when I have my camera card.

<Author>KellyZ
<Content>Love the Circle! I love the Circle hotel. Not only is it a landmark to tell your hotel from the others, it is still small enough that you can walk out of the elevator and down the steps to the sidewalk and straight across to the beach, and not far from the great spots on Waikiki! An ABC store is next door and the location is close to just about everything you'll want to do in Waikiki. The rooms are nothing special, but they are nice, clean, and they have everything you need. Get a floor higher than 5 as traffic can be a little noisy at night if you are oceanfront, but it's nothing serious. This is my second stay and I won't bother looking elsewhere...

<Author>JudySydney
<Content>Great Location I had a one night stopover in Hawaii to break up my trip home from the USA as I have a bad back and had done a lot of flying in the past 5 weeks (round the world) and didn't want to sit on a plane for 14 hours or more! But also wanted a brief look at Waikiki and not just an airport hotel. The Circle Hotel was perfect.Not a posh hotel but a good price and great location and clean! Right on the beach and along with being on the beachfront I discovered the best place to eat breakfast! (who cares that there is no restaurant in the hotel when you find something better) Just go down a couple of blocks (towards Diamond Head) past Maccas and Burger King and turn left at Kalakaua Ave. There is a restaurant there called Arancino that serves an Italian buffet breakfast for $15. It was the best buffet breakfast I had in my whole 5 weeks away! If you meet a waiter there called Marc say hi from me - he is great.Was a great one night stopover....made even better by the taxi that picked me up to go to the airport - a stretch limo!

Keep in mind I鈥檓 very petite, just imagine if you were a large person. I got the ocean view, which I admit was worth the extra money. If you are looking for a high-class hotel this is NOT it. I found the bed sheets to be a little on the sticky/dirty side. The room has a brand new flat-screen TV, which is about the only thing it had going for it. If you want a place to sleep and shower, then this is your best bargain in Wakiki Beach.The staff was friendly. There are free towels, so I thought that was pretty nice. They had limited parking available, but if you did get a rental, then the parking fee is $10/day to park. I would stay here again, but only for a few days, and no more. Overall, an excellent bargain for the budget traveler.

<Author>sapphire15
<Content>Best view for the price We stayed here for 4 nights in early May and found it just right for the two of us. (#1407 gives you a view of the Ala Moana Surfrider and the Pink Lady Hawaiian) This kitchy little hotel is directly across from a park so views of the ocean are fabulous. Free paper and coffee every morning...Until I win the lottery, I would NEVER stay anywhere else.

The front desk staff are helpful but were really only good at recommending the usual touristy eating venues!Tour desk staff were reasonably helpful.

<Author>Confusedalways
<Content>Please stay here! Ok so after days and hours of searching and researching hotels in Oahu I decided on this one. Thank God! If you were like me and frantically trying to find a good place to go, PLEASE just stop and go to this hotel!The location is the absolute best! Right across from the beach, near all the shops, resturants, the Zoo and various public bus and tour pick up points. The rooms are not THAT small! Two people fit wonderfully in the space. Three would be ok and four might be too much...unless its two adults and two kids. The trouble with space when there is more than two people is trying to find a spot for the suitcase. But if you can make good use of the closet three people is fine. There is a closet to hang up stuff (if u have a lot of stuff to hang bring more hangers). Also there is a safe inside the closet which was very useful. There is a desk to put various things on, a good flatscreen tv with regular cable tv and movies you can rent. There are two double beds. If you are a large couple you may end up sleeping in different beds. We are a small couple and even ended up in different beds just so we could roll around more comfortably. However they have put in some Queen size beds. Which are only located on the 2nd floor, so if you want a room with a view you will have to give up the Queen bed. Now the dreaded bathrooms. A lot of ppl have commented on the bathrooms in this hotel. OK so, the bathroom itself isnt that small BUT the shower I have to say is very small. There is plenty of counter space for your things and enough room to have two people putting on make up or whatnot. The shower is not made for large people at all. Iam a small girl and I bumped my elbows many times. If you want to have a nice shower together...forget it. A small shower however isnt enough not to stay here.There is some noise I must say. I requested a high up room so that we were away from street noise. The street noise was much less however the noise from the a\c machine on the building next to us got much louder. I believe no matter where you are positioned that there will be some kind of noise. I would say the least noise might be the very Oceanfront top floor but alll you have to do is keep your sliding door closed and your own ac machine on.The maid service was excellent, fresh towels everyday. Front desk did their job well, and you get beach towels when you want them. The tour desk was also very good. I must say though that one of the ladies there was very very good! I reccomend trying to book things with her (Hawaiian lady) the other lady that was there got the job done but it was like pulling teeth (Chinese lady).So all in all this is the place to be. Good price for everything you get ,very well worth it and I had a great time. A couple tips not involving the hotel. Be careful with taxis. Some taxi drivers will try and scam you by offering you the same price as public transit to take you somewhere. This just cant be right. Another tip is to take transit as much as possible. Its $2 for one way no matter how far. Booking a tour to some places that the bus can take you costs wayyyy more. Use the bus to go to diamond head and hanuma bay. Ask the tour desk, they will tell you everything and if the bus can take you there. Another tip is plan your meals. One of the biggest problems we had was figuring out what to eat. In waikiki its either fast food or expensive restuarants. We did find a few places that had good food and wasnt expensive. One place is called The Cheescake Factory. Very good place...but VERY busy. Dont go at usual meal times like 12 for lunch and 6-7 for dinner.Ok iam sure I could ramble more but I think this is good. Good luck! And have fun! Its Hawaii!  P.S wear sunscreen!

<Content>Location, location, location! This older but renovated property across the street from the Waikiki Beach has nice clean comfortable rooms that feature HD flat panel tv's, memory foam double beds, large lanai's with two chairs  a small table, and a closet with extra shelving. <Author>Tilchestuners
<Content>Ideally placed for Waikiki Beach We stayed here 14 nights over Christmas 2007.If you want a reasonably priced hotel overlooking Waikiki Beach, then this one would be hard to beat.It is, as its name suggests - a circle - a 14 or so floor tube of a tower, just over the road from Waikiki beach.The Ocean Front rooms have a splendid view of the beach and the Pacific ocean and are ideally placed to view those gorgeous Hawaiian Sunsets.The rooms are small by US standards. The twin bed rooms are as-described - Doubles - not queens - so your delight with these will depend on your normal sleeping arrangements.The, rare, Queen bed rooms seem a much better use of the space and, having tried both, we preferred the Queen bedded room.The Ocean front rooms and ocean view rooms do give the views as described. The other rooms look directly at the adjacent hotels.The hotel is situated directly in front of a nice, though busy, sandy part of Waikiki beach.The Hotel areas we visited were clean and, provided we could be sure of a Queen-bedded room, we'd be happy to return as it is, for Waikiki, and in that price range, a good location.

<Author>sredheada
<Content>Another great stay at the Circle We stayed five days. Dec 19-24, 2007 This was my second stay at this hotel. I just love this hotel. It is a small hotel. The rooms are small as are the bathrooms but who cares with the view you get and the price you pay. All the rooms now have brand new big flat screen TVs. We booked a ocean front room and the view was incredible as usual. The elevators are fast. The employees at the front desk were so friendly! They have a place outside where you can borrow boogie boards, surf boards, beach mats etc. Pleople just leave what they have bought and don't want to carry home. It was nice not to have to buy a beach mat since I only wanted to use it a few times. This hotel has no pool but who needs a pool when you have the ocean right across the street. They have big fluffy beach towels you can borrow at the front desk. The bathroom has no tub just a shower and yes the shower is small but my husband is 6'3'' and he never complained. My only slight complaint is the bathroom floor needs a good scrubbing with bleach as the grout is getting very dirty. I just put a towel on the floor and felt better. I would have liked to have been double sheeted. I'm sure I could have asked and the maid would have done it but didnt want to bother her. I think what makes this hotel so nice is that it is small and personal not like the mega resorts in the area. I highly recomend this hotel. When I return to Hawaii I will again stay at this hotel

<Author>Michelle033
<Content>Fantastic location Fantastic location. While this hotel is not the flashest in Waikiki by any stretch of the imagination, being directly accross the road from Waikiki beach, it is fantastic value for money. As per the other reviews the rooms are fairly small but how much time are you going to spend in your room anyway when the beach is calling from accross the road? <Author>scropp
<Content>Better than before! My wife and I stayed at the 'Circle' several years ago along with a short stay in another hotel, and repeated that sequence again. The Waikiki Circle was a little run down when we stayed before, but they have re-marketed themselves very successfully. Now falling into the category of a 'boutique' hotel. It looks like it never left the 60's, but in a good way. We chose an ocean front room for the excellent view. We found everything to be clean and comfortable, housekeeping was immaculate (they use 2 people working together, for speed or security I guess). The view is good from the 5th floor, but I wouldn't go any lower. The showers are still a little too small for me, but then I haven't lost any weight since my last visit so I guess that one is on me...Sitting on the balcony (lanai) watching people, the water and the sunsets. Well worth the price of admission to that show!Here's a hint: If you plan on having a car, make sure you make arrangements for parking. It is first come, first served and only $10 per day! Very small parking area under the structure.

<Author>HollywoodTravelAgent
<Content>Fantastic location, great views, helpful staff! My partner and I stayed at the Circle from November 30th thru December 3rd. The location was ideal, right in the middle of everything. The pie-shaped room was smallish as was the bathroom but who cares when you're only using the space to sleep and shower. The bed was very comfy and closet/drawer space was perfect. We had an ocean view room on the 3rd floor and it was great. If you book one of the other rooms and are offered an upgrade you should accept it. It's well worth it. The higher floors' view is much better but I'm afraid of heights and requested a lower floor.The world famous Waikiki beach is a very short walk right across the street. There are countless shops, bars, restaurants and ABC convenience stores right outside the lobby of the Circle. Your hardest decision is whether to go left or right. The shopping within walking distance ranges from cheesey tourist traps and roving carts to Louis Vuitton and Tiffany's. The eateries range from the familiar McDonald's to the raucous rooftop Tiki's Bar  Grill to very expensive and formal steak houses. My description of Waikiki is Miami meets Las Vegas...and I mean that in a good way.I've read some complaints about the parking situation and I can confirm spaces are limited. It seemed there are only spaces for about 8 to 10 cars. We had no problem finding a spot each night but our stay there was considered low season. It should also be noted the Circle does not have a pool and the onsite restaurant has been closed down for some time. But you can make arrangements with the front desk to use the pool at the adjoining ResortQuest property if you absolutely must go for a chlorine dunk rather than a dip in the warm blue sea. As for the restaurant being closed -- you won't even notice with the countless choices all over.I would highly recommend the Waikiki Circle for my clients on a mid-level budget. By the way, I took lots of pictures but decided not to post any because they look exactly like those already posted :)Aloha!

As a travel agent I've stayed at a few hotels over the years. I found the reviews to be a little generous. The staff are nice and it's hard to beat the location. <Author>PrincessKatja
<Content>Great value in a terrific location This is the place to stay if you go to Honolulu to experience Waikiki and the busy nightlife - and just sleep in your hotel. <Author>monica-TA
<Content>love this hotel This is the second time we stayed at the Circle and both times where great. The hotel is right opposite the beach ( less than 2 mins walk). The hotel has complimentary float ons. The rooms are fine for two people and are really clean. The staff at the front desk, housekeeping etc are all lovely. They all treated us like family. The hotel has been in the one family since it was built and has a long history in Waikiki. This makes you feel less like a number like at some of the other hotels. There is a complimentary paper each morning and free kona coffe in the foyer. All the rooms have flat screen TV's and are safe and secure. It is ideally located next to an ABC shop and close to McDonalds and some great restuarants like Tiki's at the aresortquest waikikii beach hotel. its a short walk to the bus stop and most of the shuttles stop 5 mins away at the Duke statue on Waikiki Beach. I recommend booking your trip to Waikele ( factory outlets) at the tour desk plus talk to them about all your tour requests - they are really helpful. I will be definately staying there again next year.

<Content>Great value, great location My wife and I recently spent two nights at Resortquest Waikiki Circle hotel. From the outside, it looks very tired and dated however the location is unbelievable. <Author>Anabel1165
<Content>BEST DEAL, BEST LOCATION This hotel is the best value for your money. It is located across the street from Waikiki Beach, next to expensive hotels. The location cannot be any better. Staff was very nice. The rooms are a bit small, but adequate for 2 or 3 people. Not luxurious, but who needs it if you will be out and about most of the day. We booked a regular room (the most economical) and we were upgraded to ocean view. It was the best. There is a free night show across the street every night we were there and we just sat outside of our balcony to see it. The hotel offers free use of their beach toys, which is great when traveling with children. There is a McDonalds and ABC Store next door. I saw some very expensive hotels located 1 or 2 blocks away with no ocean view like this one and I could just imagine their cost. This is the best value. I will definetely stay here again. Also the parking is so economical ($10/day) compared to the hotels next door (almost $30/day). You can't go wrong. You will save a lot of money to wine and dine in wakiki instead.

<Author>RobynW
<Content>Loved it!! This is a budget hotel (so don't expect fancy) but for the price it has to be the best place to stay on Waikiki Beach. Rooms: clean, small, upgrade to oceanview. Perfect size for two people (3 would be tight). I would suggest floors 5 and above to get the best view. Truly, the rooms are not fancy but they provide everything you need.Staff: very friendly and helpful. The staff at the excursions desk was particularly good.Amenities: parking right there. Floats, boogie boards, surf boards are all right at the front entrance and you just grab them and cross the street to the beach. Very handy!!! ABC store right next door as well as a McDonalds. Coffee in the lobby every morning.Beach: very nice, directly across from the hotel is a very protected swim area within a sea wall, to the right and left are more open areas of beach. For a change, walk down towards the Honolulu Zoo (5 minutes) and there is beach in front of a beautiful park with great shade trees. It's a nice change from laying on sand.Excursions: nothing to do with the hotel but FYI we booked several excursions through Hawaii Activities (online). 1. Kailua Kayaking tour was nothing special, I woudn't spend the money on it. 2. If you are truly interested in WW2 history book the Pearl Harbor Home of the Brave tour (Pearl, Wheeler Field, Schofield Barracks, Fort Shafter with lunch at the Officer's Club, Punch Bowl Cemetary and Home of the Brave Museum). It's awesome.3. We hiked Manoa Falls (breathtaking) and Diamond Head (go early in the morning, we had no crowds). Warning about Manoa Falls--apparently it's usually dry this time of year (we got lucky because of the hurricane which brought some rain to make it flow). 4. Hawaii Shark Encounter was the coolest thing I've ever done. My 10 year old and I did it. Highly recommended. 5. The Honolulu Zoo and the Aquarium are a 5 minute walk from the hotel. Both were great.I would definitely stay at the Waikiki Circle again. Completely adequate accomodation, great location, great price!

<Author>kasey363
<Content>1st timer  1st timer to Hawaii and 1st timer to use of a travel service (Pleasant Holidays) so that is how I found this ResortQuest property. I hope my 1st time to the Waikiki Circle will not be my last - I'd make this hotel my choice if staying in Oahu again.I'll second many reviews here with these essentials from my seven day stay:If you are 2-3 people in one room, appreciate cleanliness, helpful service from office staff  housekeeping (suggestions to local eats, extra towels requested and received everyday, generous with soaps and shampoos etc, smile and aloha spirit consistently every day), plenty of beach toys, boogie boards and surf boards and beach towles to use; if you love a central location to restaurants, shopping, activity centers, and of course Wakiki beach and all it has to offer....this is the place! Parking is right there and never had a problem - they even have extra parking at sister prop next door if there is an overflow.If you haven't already - take the upgrade (for $60.00 for one week when we check in they asked) and get a full front ocean view. We had the 11th floor - it was fantastic....no noise, the lanai was our central place for breakfasts, people watching and snacks/drinks under the stars. Sunrise and sunsets....beautiful.Yes the bathroom is small. Believe me - you can deal. Flush, wash, brush and shower - how long are you in there anyway?Rooms are clean. Beds are comfortable. Closet space is adequate (we had six bags and did just fine - you have floor space in room). Safe in closet - like a $2.00 fee a day - small price for peace of mind. Refer a plus, small but you drink and eat everyday or so, so just step outside and restock - ABC stores and Foodland/Big Save supermarkets abound!New wide screen flat TV's just installed - I think we had it on like five minutes each day (to see it rain back home in the Northeast HA!)....see the island instead! Elevators worked just fine - no slowness or breakdowns. Rooms were quiet - no room to room noise. Yes there is no restaurant on site - but there are like 400 around you, yes there is no pool, but - uh....the Pacific is right across the street and it's the biggest pool you can imagine! Even have a calm kiddie pool (walled breakwater - directly across the street) for you that like it calm. If that's not enough beach for you - go left - go right - plenty.Consider this:Beautiful viewsIn the center of Waikiki action and conveninceWalk across the street in your bathing suit and - go swimming, boogieboarding, surfing, outrigger canoe rides, catamaran sails, see the free shows (hula/music etc).Walk a few blocks to the right and go to the zoo, botanical gardens, parks, more beaches, more shopping, more food.Walk a few blocks to the left and do it all over again with different beaches, eats, stores, parks.Drive a mile and hike Diamond Head. Drive a mile and be on Highway 1 East or West your access to anywhere on Oahu.15 minutes on HW1 to Pearl Harbor, Honolulu sites (Iaoni Palace, Chinatown, Aloha Tower, Airport etc). 10 minutes on HW 1 to Napali Highway and explore East Oahu. Coastal Drive right past Diamond Head - keep exploring! North Shore....PCC...it's all doable from easy access and believe me - traffic is NOT that bad on highways or in Waikiki. Take it from this Boston/NYC vicinity life - this is NOT traffic. You are in Oahu - Waikiki - vacation.....take in the sights, sounds and smells - chill out in steady 80 degree temps, then sit on your lanai in the PM and watch the waves.... The next time can't come fast enough. This is a great spot.

<Author>chacco
<Content>Not bad for the price Just came back from a 5 night stay at this hotel. As other reviewers have stated, the rooms are definitely small, but it's doable for two people. The size of the bathroom is equivalent to those of the cruise ships'. As an average-sized person, I banged my arms against the wall every day while showering. Our oceanview room had a view of half the ocean which to me should really be considered a partial oceanview. There was some paint peeling from the ceiling. This hotel charges for using the in-room safe which still uses a key lock instead of a combination lock. But overall, the hotel was not bad for the price we paid. It's conveniently located with the beach across the street, restaurants and shops nearby and the bus stop just a block away on Kuhio Ave. If you just need basic accommodation with a nice view, this is the place. If you want something fancy, look elsewhere.

<Author>PurpleZoe21
<Content>Clean, basic, good accommodation We stayed at the Circle for 3 nights in April. I choose this hotel from brochures because of the location and the price. I was a little disappointed when I first arrived. The rooms are quite small and getting a bit tired. But they were clean - the bathroom clean and the linen on the bed clean and fresh. However you can't see Diamond Head. When you are sitting on the balcony (we were on the western side) all you can hear is the air conditioner from the building below (very annoying!)The location of this hotel is perfect - straight across the road is a great swimming beach and you have all the shops you need within walking distance.I wouldn't stay here again, I would choose another hotel that was maybe a three or four stay. But hey, if you don't really care for 'all the extras' it would make a great place to stay.

<Content>We will be back in heartbeat! LOVED this hotel. While it's not one the fanciest and could be one of the smallest...you canNOT beat the location, the view and even the staff! The value compared to other beachfront hotels is second to none...why would you pay more for a beach front fancy hotel when this Waikiki Circle has the same beach front?! We also upgraded for a minimal price to a beachfront room and the view was AMAZING. Sure, rooms may not be as spacious as other hotels, but who cares!? The view people, the view! Shower is small but bed is comfy. Room is small, but we used the other bed as a luggage rack. We made it work. The hotel did not seem crowded at all and we never had to wait for an elevator. The first night for parking we had to park at their sister hotel which was about 3 blocks away, but they told us to call the front desk first thing the next morning and they would save us a spot in their parking lot. So we called the next morning and got it. Easy as pie. I was surprised at how easy it was! Seriously, for the value and location, you cannot go wrong at this place. You are in HAWAII, you shouldn't be holed up in your room anyways! As long as there is a bed and shower, that's all you need. We will be back and we are so glad we choose this hotel.

<Author>donyandell
<Content>Really is Oceanfront! The Resortquest Waikiki Circle hotel is an older property, and has small bathrooms, but it makes up for it in its location and view!We had two rooms (803  805), which were both oceanfront. I recommend that you ask for rooms that are -04 (e.g. 804, 1004). They are direct oceanfront. Our two rooms had a slight angle, and were not quite as nice as the -04 room. However, rooms that are 03-05 in number have incredible views (The 05 room would be second choice!). Go to the hotel's website. They offer e-special rates that are the lowest prices available.The rooms all have double-beds. The staff was very kind to bring up a rollaway, extra blankets and sheets, with no additional charge. In fact, the staff was very profesional, helpful, knowledgeable, etc.The bathrooms are the size of bathrooms on cruise ships. There is no tub, just a shower. However, even for a big guy, such as myself, it was fine. The air-conditioning was a small window unit. You might want to run it continuously to have it comfortable at night (Close the full-length window curtains while you're out). You will enjoy sitting out on the lanai. It's quite a view!There is no coffee maker in the room. However, in the outdoor lobby, they have coffee every morning, beginning at 7:00 A.M. There is a mini-fridge in the rooms. In-room safes are available, but cost (I think about $2.50 a night). Just outside the lobby (to your right) is an ABC convenience store that has everything you would need and want. Outside the lobby to your left is a McDonalds. Both are only 10-20 steps away. There are stores and restaurants up-and-down the street.Parking is underground, and costs $9.00 per night. That's a bargain, considering other hotels!We loved the hotel, and plan to stay there the next time we visit Oahu.

<Author>ToniVitanza
<Content>Loved the Circle! I'm a 45-year-old female flight attendant who has visited Hawaii many times with my family over the last ten years. I've stayed at Aston/ResortQuest hotels most of those visits. This was my first time at the Waikiki Circle. We stayed the first week of November and I doubt we will ever stay anywhere else in Waikiki! Judging from the other reviews, the Circle doesn't really need me to chime in with praise, but here goes.Very cool, groovy and retro. Cheap, cheerful, clean and fun. Location CANNOT be beat. Waikiki is JUST across the street, the Circle has sweet yellow umbrellas on the sand for guests and water toys in a rack just off the open-air lobby.We had two rooms, one for my parents (first-timers) and one for myself, my husband and our 13-year-old son. A tip: Pay the extra $10 or so and get a room higher up. It will be quieter and you will have a better view of the ocean. The elevators are fast enough and the view and quiet will be great!Yes, as other reviewers mention, the rooms are small. If you are the person whose body spreads into mine when sitting next to me in the economy cabin, you aren't going to like the shower. But you are hardly going to Hawaii to enjoy a luxurious room. The little desk by the mirrored closet is an ideal addition to the counterspace in the bathroom. If you have room in your bag, bring a great BIG fluffy towel for beach and bathroom use. As soon as you enter, open those curtains!!! Enjoy your lanai. (Ideal for smokers.) And remember what you paid. First thing after you've opened those curtains, plug in your refrigerator. The maids leave it unplugged to save electricity. Plug it in ASAP for your leftovers and drinks.Les was great at the front desk, and the staff was great about calling a cab for us a couple of times and also more than happy to store our bags after the noon checkout on the last day, giving us the opportunity to spend time around Waikiki before heading for our early-evening flight. The lady at the tour desk in the lobby was wonderful, gave us great advice about our visit to Pearl Harbor and arranged a very inexpensive transport to and from there. My one complaint, and it is a little one, is about the complimentary coffee service in the lobby. Most mainlanders in Hawaii get up early (and consequently poop out early) when in the islands due to the jet lag. 7:30 or 8:00 a.m. is too late for complimentary coffee to be very meaningful. I would suggest putting it out earlier if you truly want your guests to enjoy it. There was not a single morning when we did not avail ourselves of coffee at either McDonald's or at the Kona coffee kiosk in front of the Pacific Hotel (both just steps away from the Circle's lobby) because the lobby's coffee wasn't out yet. We then simply walked across the street and enjoyed it on the beach. I have told many a passenger: You will wake up early, and this is a blessing. Get up, slide your feet into your flip-flops and walk on that beach when the moon is still up and there is no one there but you and the local with the fishing pole or geiger-counter. Enjoy the beach this way in the morning because by 9 am it's a riot of people.Caveats: I almost hate to say any of this, but....the Waikiki Circle is NOT a honeymoon/romance type of hotel. There are no king (or even queen) sized beds, no hot tub, no pool, no room service, not even a bath tub in the room (shower only). This is an IDEAL girlfriend getaway or familymoon place. Unbelievable value. If you think you'll never go to Waikiki because you just can't afford the hotel rates, this is the place for you. I can give reams of advice about Hawaii and specifically Waikiki, but, in a nutshell:In the Waikiki area, visit Cheeseburger in Paradise for a meal and a great t-shirt. We never miss at least one breakfast at the Oceanarium buffet at the Pacific Hotel, but the breakfast buffet at Duke's Canoe Club gave it a run for its money this time around. Everyone knows to visit Pearl Harbor their first time in Honolulu, but make an effort to go to Iolani Palace too, a bus ride away in downtown Honolulu and excellent if it's rainy or overcast. An awesome tour for $20 a head, or get an audio for a lot less, but DO GO. It will help to have a rudimentary, 10-minutes-on-the-internet history lesson before you go, if you can't do any more homework than that. We have climbed Diamond Head as a family, taken a picture, and made our son promise to take the same picture with his family someday. Get a cab or bus ride to the entrance to the trail if you're up for that. It's fun to sit on the beach with your drink, look at Diamond Head, and know you've been to the top. We always spring for ONE expensive round of drinks at the beach bar behind the Sheraton Surfrider (the gingerbread hotel, you can't miss it) and we will never miss an evening at the Halekulani Hotel's beach bar, called House Without A Key. (Tell the cab driver to take you to the Halekulani, say Holly-koo-lonny, down the street. It's a cheap ride, don't try to walk.) At 5 pm a Grammy-nominated band starts playing on the beach, at 6 the hula dancer begins her program (a former Miss Hawaii). Get there early for a good spot. Very romantic and old-world Hawaii. Order the coconut shrimp with your drinks and watch the sun set behind the band. We always enjoy an inexpensive Thai meal at Keoni's, near the Princess Kaiulani Hotel (people will point you there). They have an inexpensive breakfast menu too, traditional American fare. There is a coffee place in the front part of the Surfrider, you can sit in the gingerbread window with your mate and it makes a great photo from the sidewalk, if you can get someone to snap it. The coffee is fabulous, esp. with the mango pastry. I love other spots in the Hawaiian Islands more, but my husband is a nut for the action and activity of Waikiki. He says he doesn't want to stay anywhere else from now on but the Waikiki Circle. My parents agree that if they go back to Waikiki, it's where they'll stay as well.  
<Date>Nov 26, 2006

<Author>Mehune
<Content>Great place to sleep  hotel is on same street as int'l marketplace and tons of restaurants and shops--its basically where all the hotels are. we didn't have to drive at all at nite to dinner or shopping. only took the car out to go to non-waikiki beaches (every day except first and last) and to airport.when you go to oahu (without children), you only need a room to dump your stuff, shower after swimming, and sleep. this hotel is PERFECT for that. DON'T expect a spa/resort and you will NOT be disappointed!! the rooms are all the same size, all have double beds and balconies, and are pie shaped. TINY rooms, but unless you're going to be ballroom dancing in the room, who cares??all the drawbacks of the facility are NO big deal, if you are going to oahu for what you SHOULD be going for: swimming, shopping, eating, drinking, and having FUN!! drawbacks: no pool but who needs one when your hotel is across the street from the best part of waikiki beach; no restaurant but don't need one on the street FULL of places to eat; varying degrees of crankiness from hotel staff but who cares you don't talk to them except to ask for as many towels as you want; tiny pkg lot but we always got a spot; slightly dingy street and icky people (some hookers!) but after 24 hrs i didn't even notice that...the pluses WAY outweigh any and all of these minuses. i am a VERY picky person, did LOADS of research about everything prior, and i recc this hotel. as aforementioned, don't expect a seaside couples massage or a mint on your pillow but do expect very diligent cleaning service (she even gave us extra towels w/o asking) and adequate accomodations. don't fall for the discount rate for a viewed room. why do you need a room with a view when you are across street from the beach? don't waste your money. DO fall for the discount if offerred a convertible for your rental car SO worth it!DO eat at: duke's across street, cheesecake factory (which we resisted since we have those in california but it was EXCELLENT after the hour long wait), and DO eat breakfast at Da Big Kahuna on Kuhio, one street away from the beach side. excellent hawaiian bfast. we had corned beef hash and white rice EVERY morning!! sounds gross but YUMMMMMY!!lastly: we shopped at ABC stores like, twice or thrice a day every single day and all i can say is if you think you should buy something there, DO IT cuz once you get home, you can't get it, can you?? i did TONS of christmas shopping there as 10 bucks spent there is equivalent to loads more mainland!! lastly, remember as long as your hotel is safe and clean, you will LOVE your vacation in PARADISE unless you have a stick up something...!!!!!!!!!!!!!! if you don't have fun there, there's no hope for you whatsoever!!  
<Date>Nov 25, 2006

<Author>buffettgirl
<Content>Clean and convenient It's starting to sound redundant now, but I'll go ahead and add my two cents......this is the perfect hotel for those of you who, like me, don't want to spend a fortune on accommodations but don't want to stay in a dump either. This hotel is not fancy at all but it is nowhere close to being a dump. It's clean, affordable, and incredibly convenient. The rooms and bathrooms are small (it did remind me a little of a cruise ship cabin) but perfectly ample for two. The location is fantastic; right in the heart of Waikiki Beach. The staff is friendly. The beach towels they loan you are huge and fluffy. I thought the bed was very comfortable; I think the most comfortable hotel bed I've ever slept in. I had a partial ocean view, so I could not see Diamond Head from my balcony, but I could see the beach and the waves. And I kind of liked being able to also see the hustle and bustle of Honolulu on the other side. If you are like me and like to get and do things on vacation rather than hang out at the hotel, I highly recommend this one. (Otherwise no; there is no pool and limited services.)

<Author>Bebeeann
<Content>Excellent location! We stayed at the hotel Sept 30th thru October 2nd before going on a cruise. We chose this hotel after reading all of the other hotel reviews. I can say that we were very happy with our choice. You cannot beat the location and we also upgraded to an ocean front room for $20 additional a night and do not regret it. As others have commented, the shower is extremely small (smaller than the shower on our Carnival cruise ship) but it was fine for what we needed. The beds were great, we slept so well. The hotel does not have a lobby, but we found the staff extremely helpful and they also recommended Dukes to us, and we loved the food and atmosphere. I strongly recommend dining there. The ABC stores are everywhere and it was nice to have the McDonalds so close. We sat on our balcony watched the sunsets and listened to the music being performed across the street in the park. It was very nice. It is so close to the beach, it was so easy to walk to the beach come back if we forgot something or wanted a snack. The hotel also provided beach towels which was very nice and greatly appreciated. We also used the beach toys which the hotel provided. There was no need to purchase a raft or anything other type of toy. One of the elevators went out of service when we were there but it was fixed the next day. The travel desk was very helpful and spent a lot of time with us. I recommend getting an ocean front room higher than the 5th floor. We were on the 5th floor and would have preferred to be a bit higher. The only bad thing that I have to say is that the air conditioners are single window units in the wall and sometimes depending on how the wind blew, condensation water would drip on you from the air conditioner. Also, there was a lot of road noise, but the view made it all worth it! Overall the room was clean, beds were great and you cannot beat the location or view! I don't know if we would have stayed there if our final desination was Oahu since there is no pool or other ammenities that you find at other hotels, but for the price.......it cannot be beat! I would recommend this hotel to family and friends and we would stay there again. Happy travels!  
<Date>Oct 17, 2006

<Content>Best View And Value. This Is Waikiki'S Hidden Treasure! This is the best hotel I have stayed in with regard to its value. The staff was incredibly friendly always competent and very knowledgeable of not only Waikiki but Oahu and the neighbor islands as well. Every restaurant recommendation from Ciao Mein (yes italian and chinese) to lunch at the nearby swanky Kahala were right on the mark. This hotel is superbly run. 2. <Author>kahuna1959
<Content>best location for the price We stayed here for two nights on our way back home from the Big Island. The hotel location is fantastic for the price. Value-wise it's hard to beat this hotel. It is directly across from the main beach at Waikiki. An ABC store on one side of the main entrance for incidentals and a McDonalds on the other side for a fast breakfast on your way out!. Coffee down at the front desk in the morning is very good quality. The front desk staff were very knowlegable and I asked for their help several times for driving directions etc. The rooms are small but if you are two adults traveling together there is plenty of room. If you are two adults with two children you will be cramped. There is a small fridge in the room which we found very helpful. The views from the lanai, even the city view rooms, are still decent if you are on the upper floors. Staying up higher also gets you out of the noise from the street and traffic. My only real complaints are that it would be nice to have a pool for an evening cool-down, and they don't have nearly enough parking for hotel guests on site. The heat in July was a bit more than we expected and we didn't want to go to the beach in the late evening. We had a car because we wanted to get out of Waikiki and see the less populated areas and beaches. We had to park at another hotel a few blocks away for one night. The next day they made room for us outside the lobby area at no charge to help us out which was very nice of them. For the money? GREAT DEAL! I'd go back tomorrow.  
<Date>Aug 4, 2006

<Content>Rooms okay for two We stayed for two nights plus had a late check out on day 3. Our group of 5 adults had 2 rooms on the 13th floor. Or blow a conch at sunset!Room fridge great for bottled water, snacks  alcohol beverages. We had an ancient A/C  TV, but our 'other room' had new ones. Would stay here again only in a pinch.

<Author>Elzed
<Content>Very Ordinary We stayed at this hotel for a total of 5 nights (4 consecutive and 1 later in our trip). Whilst the hotel has position, position, position (great views of the beach if you are lucky enough to have a beach view room), it really has not much else to offer. The rooms are comfortable but very small and hot and noisy. The alternatives for sleeping at night are to leave the balcony door open (too noisy from the street noise and other air conditioners) or to leave the old-fashioned air conditioner running all night and neither is ideal for a good night's sleep. The bathrooms are also quite small and in one of the rooms we had the paint was peeling off the wall in places.There are no dining facilities, no room service and no coffee making facilities either apart from being able to get a cup of coffee from the foyer for a short time in the morning. Fortunately there are plenty of places to dine in the street. This hotel is fine if you want just basic accommodation but if you are expecting a little more then this is not the place.

<Author>Ants48
<Content>Great place to stay! Stayed at the Circle for 10 nights in February and we had a great time. We were hesitant on booking this place because of the negative reviews we had read but we were more than pleased with our choice and the ocean view from the lanai was superb. The room itself was a little on the small side and the bathroom was rather tight, but this was expected. We did not have a major problem with the water pressure as others have noted, although it could have been a little better. As for the shower, it would be a little tight for anybody who could be considered a larger size, although I did not have a problem with it. On the plus side, apart from the sensational view was the brilliant location right across the street from a great stretch of swimmable beach, and the close proximity to a fantastic selection of shops and restaurants. The staff were all very friendly and being a small hotel the service was very personable. I would recommend the Circle if you are interested in a clean but smallish room in a brilliant location and do not wish to spend a fortune.

<Author>biogirl
<Content>Great location! I was a bit leery when I booked this hotel originally because of some bad reviews, but we were pleasantly surprised when we got there. The hotel is directly in front of the beach, with views that are just as good as any of the 5 star hotels. However, you get what you pay for - the rooms are tiny. With just 2 of us we were comfortable, but the bathroom was tiny, specifically the shower. We had a partial ocean view room that had a gorgeous view on the diamond head side, and were on the 13th floor. We took advantage of the balcony and sat out on it almost every day.Though we were so high up Waikiki is noisy at night! We probably should have closed the door at night, but we liked it open. There is free coffee in the lobby every morning. We had no problems with the elevators, and the place was kept very clean. Also, we requested a non-smoking room - I'm not even sure if they have them, as are room was equipped with ashtrays, but there was no lingering smell or anything. One thing that I didn鈥檛 like was that they charged 75 cents per outgoing call, whether it was local or using a calling card 鈥?which was a pain to try and make reservations and call home using a payphone on the beach.It鈥檚 also close to the action, short walk to many different restaurants and shops, and close to the international marketplace. No pool, but there was only one really windy day when we gave up on the beach that we would have used it if we had one. We usually camped out in front of the Moana Surfrider and relaxed (this is the place we want to stay next time we go to Hawaii when we have more money!). Also, they gave us a coupon book when we checked in that was useful (free cheesecake from Tikis!).Overall it was a great place if you are on a budget, probably not good if you are planning on having 4 people stay in the room 鈥?would be cramped. But we enjoyed it and were happy with our choice for our first trip to Hawaii.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Motel 6 Of Waikiki The only pro about this hotel is that it is located at the heart of waikiki across from the beach. If you are planning on being out all day and have an extremely tight budget and are only concerned about getting a few hours of sleep after a long day of exploration, then maybe this is the hotel for you.You will quickly learn that you better have a long day and night planned since there are minimal guest services and amenities at your disposal at this rat hole. Please remember that this hotel is a converted boarding house for troops during WWII. There is no pool (what resort doesn't have a pool to chill out in after swimming in the ocean all day? after all this is RESORTQUEST waikiki right?), no central AC, the bathroom is oddly divided so that the sink and mirror are separated from the toilet and shower (water pressure is a trickle). There are no extra pillows or towels conveniently available should a need arise for them and the front desk personnel are quick to remind you that this hotel is indeed appropriately rated two stars with curt and rude remarks about how we don't have people to run errands like that, you'll have to come down here and get it yourself (thanks, jan, you're super sweet). so why complain? i'm not complaining, i'm giving a review. this hotel was recommended to us by travel agents who made grave misrepresentations. if you want to relax and enjoy yourself go to kaua'i or one of the other islands and stay clear of waikiki and the waikiki circle hotel. it's less commercialized and the concept of aloha is better preserved on the other islands and in other establishments than in waikiki and the waikiki circle hotel.

<Author>rf0
<Content>Best location on the beach at great price Just returned from a stay at the Circle. Here are the good points-Absolutely great location, oceanfront rooms truly oceanfront with best view on Waikiki. Located directly across one street to the sand. Walk to beach is as short as the other hotels charging outrageous prices. Nice central location to shops, restaurants etc. Our room on the 9th floor was very clean, no smoke smell. Decorated very cute. Small fridge and good coffee in lobby area. Elevators work very fast and smooth. Employees were much more friendly than the average we met in Waikiki. Now for the not so good points for some people-The rooms are small by some standards. But there was a nice closet and it was large enough for us. The balcony is large and that is where I sat to read etc. Who stays in the room anyway? No tub, and shower is small-but not a problem for us. I learned that unless you plan to drive everyday-it is not worth the cost of renting a car daily, if you are staying at the Circle and doing the Waikiki thing. You are located walking distance to just about everything and there are numerous trolleys and buses cheap! Just get a car for when you intend on traveling the island. The rental cars have locations close to the Circle, plus I think they will deliver.We are country, farm people and Waikiki is not for us-very busy and the beach was crowded this time of year. But we did enjoy the view very much from our room. I am so thankful that we did stay at the Circle and had the nice balcony and view. If we have to stay in town again, we will definitely stay at the Circle again. I will try to post later about the places we visited and the rest of our stay at Kailua and Lanikai. If you are looking for a quiet area, please feel free to email me.

<Author>bagherra
<Content>Not a good place for non-smokers When my husband and I are discussing ther merits of differenct places we have stayed, this is our benchmark of icky. We booked a non-smoking room. When we checked in there was actually visible smoke issuing from the vent in the bathroom. We were adjacent to a smoking room and the circulation system ensures that all rooms are smoking rooms. We were offered another room, same problem and then rebooked into the Aston Waikiki Beach just a few block down the same street, which was fine. The staff was very nice about it, and I got the impression this is a common problem. This hotel caters to smokers and has an elderly air circulation system. If you are not prepared to accept a seriously smoky environment, don't stay here. Rooms were tiny and bathrooms tinier. I am 5'0 and my husband is 5'6, so we usually never even notice the height of the shower. I think that is the first shower we have ever seen that was too short for us. I had an overall impression of dirtiness, which to be fair was probably influenced by the overwhelming smell of tobacco. Since we were just down the street, we walked by often and noticed many people partying on the balconies, sort of a college dorm atmosphere with lots and lots of cigarettes, so if that is your cup of tea, you might be pleased by this place. The location is excellent, but the cigarette smoke was beyond belief.

<Content>Perfect for us! This hotel is awesome if you are on a budget yet want to be practically on the beach with awesome views! When we got to the room we opened the curtains and about died and went to heaven! The door/window fills the whole room! We had an oceanfront room but I am sure the partial ocean rooms would be pretty good too! There are two queen beds (I think they were) and me and my hubby decided to sleep separetly because they were a bit small and we aren't big people but we like are space! The room is small but it is a circular hotel as well. The only thing that I didn't really like about the room was the bathroom. The shower was almost too small for one person (but doable). The beds were o.k. to sleep on. Not too hard... but don't try to have s-- on the bed because there is no give and you can't move and the springs go into your back :-) You have to pay like $2.50 a day to use their in-room safe which is really stupid! There is a desk to write on and the closet has shelving and was nice.The help at the desk was very friendly. The balcony was nice and large. I wish they had chairs you could lay down in instead. Some birds visited us out there. We slept with the door open about every night and it was really nice. <Author>Vada
<Content>Waikiki Circle Up to Expectations Having read many positive and some negative reports on the Resortquest Waikiki Circle Hotel, we found that it was up to our expectations, September -October '05. Tripadvisor resarch had prepared us for the small shower recess, little bit of paint peeling off the wall and the small rooms. However, the little bit of extra money to have the clean, oceanfront room with an absolutely FANTASTIC view was more than ample compensation. Friends who were staying in the nearby, very expensive Outrigger were extremely jealous of the size of our balcony and view. The hotel staff were efficient, friendly. Free ice for a pre-dinner duty free was a nice touch! Only down side, was the $2.60 per day fee for using the in-room safe (unusual) and the downright unfriendliness of the lady at the tour desk, after a couple of rebuffs from her we used the tour desk at the Outrigger, who were helpful, friendly and efficent. Further note; the Japanese restaurant in the foyer of the hotel is something to be avoided. On entering we were told we only serve noodles we that's ok to be greeted with  you won't like it here! We left. The restaurant is always full of Japanese, perhaps this is just a form of racial discrimination in reverse?

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Not too Shabby This Hotel has everything you would expect from a 3 star hotel. If you expect more you may be disappointed. My wife and I stayed here for the first night of our Honeymoon. We stayed in an ocean view room on the 10th floor. The view was wonderful and the location was great. It's just a short walk to the beach, a restaurant, or a bar. The rooms wont fit more than two people comfortably but you can try. The positives were the price, location, and view. The only negative was the parking. They have a parking lot but I think it only fits 3 cars. You will most likely have to park several blocks away in another hotel parking garage. The walk is about 10 minutes which isn't bad unless your one of those people that needs to run to your car all the time. I'd stay here again for a short trip. Anything more than a few days and I might look for a larger room and a closer parking lot.

<Author>beachgirl13
<Content>Great view but dirty My family, husband and daughter stayed at the Circle for 10 days. As soon as I walked in the door I knew immediately it was not the hotel for us. The bathroom was gross. The balcony floor was so black I couldn't walk barefoot. Pigeon poop all over the place. I was not able to upgrade to another Aston hotel, all booked. The company that I booked my vacation with, Expedia does not give any refunds after you arrive. So I was stuck. Went to the Food pantry bought some clorox and sprayed the bathroom floor. The towel I used to clean was literally black with dirt. Gross! Shower also did not drain. I had to call downstairs they did come up to repair. Towels are very, very small it is hard to dry off completely. Don't get me wrong I was not obsessed and didn't do all of the cleaning the first hour I was there but I was very disappointed with the room. We did have an awesome vacation otherwise. This was not going to ruin our vacation, we had a great time. Best one out of the three times we have gone. Good things to report were staff was friendly, water toys to use, front desk let me look at several other rooms, elevators were fast and like everyone says the view is to die for and the sunsets are absolutely beautiful! If I had to choose between a view with a dirty room or a clean room without a view, I would choose a clean room without a view. So next year will be a different hotel. Aloha!

<Author>anony
<Content>Great view and location We stayed in an oceanview room, and for the price, the view was awesome. We could open up the curtain and have a nice panorama of waikiki beach while lying bed. I also found the fish motif cute. The other nice thing is there is a hula performance each evening across the street from the hotel, and though our view was blocked by the banyan tree, we could open the lanai door and listen to the music while getting ready for dinner. The rooms are small, but there was just two of us so we are able to use the other bed to store our second suitcase and spread out our belongings. Everything in the room was clean and well maintained, except mattresses weren't the most comfortable I've ever slept on. The bathrooms counters/toilet/sink were in good repair. The shower stall is small, and had just a curtain. If, like me, you like to adjust the water temperature before fully stepping into the shower, you will end up with a wet floor. Also some areas around the door were rusty, and there was peeling on the shower ceiling. But to me this was not enough to ruin my experience.If you don't need all the amenities of a resort or want a luxury experience, and want an oceanview room without paying through the nose, the Circle will work for you.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>A Great Family Place! My family of seven just returned from a six night's stay at the Circle. My 70+ parents, my husband and myself, plus our three children, ages 8, 4 and 2, shared two adjacent ocean front rooms on the tenth floor. The staff were extremely accomodating. Within minutes of checking in, we received extra towels delivered to our room at no request and one of the front office staff went out of her way to make sure all my children received their Children stay, play and eat free cards and necklaces - there was only one necklace available upon check in, but she kept looking and provided two more on day #2 because she wanted to keep things fair for all three kids - she also gave us an extra bucket and shovel because she knew we only had one per room, yet three kids. Other extra, unexpected perks included: huge unlimited beach towels provided each day - we could take them anywhere on the island; free use of water toys, including rafts, surf and boogie boards, sand toys, chairs and umbrelllas; free local paper delivered to our door each morning, and a latte stand just around the corner. (My parents enjoyed the complimentary morning coffee, but my husband and I had to splurge; after all, we were on vacation) The rooms were clean and comfortable and not at all cramped, even with our huge family. The layout of the rooms worked very well and the kids had enough space to spread out - they even had room to play hide-n-seek. The panoramic view, to echo other reviews, was breathtaking. We were always drawn to sit out on the balcony so perhaps that's what made the room feel spacious - it seemed to extend out to the ocean! We were so close to the water that we were able to take in a swim each day - even on days that we went out sightseeing. And the beach directly across from the hotel was perfect for the little ones - very shallow and calm, even for my 2-year old. And talk about convenience! I loved being able to pop down to the variety stores for any little thing I needed and having a McDonald's and Jack in the Box right below helped out when the kids needed a quick, familiar bite to eat. We had a rental mini-van and never had any problems finding a parking place, even when we came and went throughout the day. All-in-all, we were thrilled with our choice of hotels. Beach access, the view, convenience, and the staff's Aloha spirit will bring us back to the Circle anytime we plan to stay on Oahu!  
<Date>Jul 17, 2005

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>great location! Our family group of 6 just returned from a seven night stay at the Circle. If I was going to return to Oahu or was going to recommend a hotel to someone going there, I would definitely consider the Circle as a unique, friendly, and well located place to stay. The staff was helpful anytime we needed directions, a recommendation for dinner or extra towels. We had a partial-ocean view, but from our lanai we could see Waikiki beach right across the street. The rooms are small, there are two double beds in each. Smaller than what I am used to(for two people to sleep in)but everything was clean and the air conditioning was efficient if needed. Over all, a great value for your vacation $$$ .

<Author>VickidFt_Myers_Fl_
<Content>Think of the price - you'll love the value I am always a little surprised when I see reviews about the Circle where people were totally unhappy.I think this is definitely a get what you pay for scenario. There is a reason the Circle is a third of the price of other hotels. The rooms are small, and old BUT.... the view is outstanding, the location absolutely cannot be beat, the lobby staff have got to be some of the nicest folks I have ever met and at this price you can afford to stay more days than you would at the Sheraton's or Hilton's of Waikiki.If older and small is not your cup of tea, and you can afford it, by all means check out other motels. But - if you want one of the best values on Waikiki - within walking distance of the zoo, shopping, fine restaurants and right across the beach from a free show, you cannot beat the Circle.

<Author>bemyguest
<Content>Hold your nose and look at the view It was Aloha Week in Honolulu. The plane landed hours late.At two am we checked in and found the hotel room smelled.Holding my nose I opened the door to the terrace and just wentto bed.Thinking the next morning we would check out other hotels andjust move on.Every other hotel was booked. And the price of an ocean-view roomwas 16 times the cost we were paying for ours.So we went to the ABC store and bought a lot of cans of air spray.None of it worked -except to make the smell worse.It short we keep the terrace door open and stayed out therewhenever we could.The big Aloha parade passed by right under our terrace. They sang and danced their way up the ocean side street toward Diamond Head--which we could clearly see day or night.And best of all I heard the late Loyal Gardner sing at an outdoor concert.If you do not know her-- find her recordings. Her range,voice and aloha spirit were unmatched.My stay was over ten years ago and I know that the hotel has undergone a complete re-do and has sentthe bad smells away.The view remains and if you check out the cost of the big hotels just across the street you will see just what that view is worth.You can put the rest of the money into your food budget.The cost now for the Circle is about 5 times what I spent then --but I would go back to the Circle in a heart beat. This is great (view) value for money.
